                                     <p style="text-align: center;">Enthought Canopy provides a <a href="/product/canopy/#/package-index">proven scientific and analytic Python package distribution</a> plus key integrated tools for iterative data analysis, data visualization, and application development.&nbsp;Users&nbsp;have the ability to extend and innovate with scripting and open platform APIs, driving the creation and sharing of innovative workflows, tools, and applications.</p>

                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <h2 style="text-align: center;">Why Canopy is the Python Platform of Choice for Scientists and Engineers</h2>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                    </div>
                                   </div>
                                   <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 30px;"></div>
                                   <div class="vc_row wpb_row section vc_row-fluid vc_inner " style=" text-align:left;">
                                    <div class=" full_section_inner clearfix">
                                     <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6">
                                      <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                       <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                        <div class="wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center  element_from_left">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <div class="vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey">
                                           <img width="400" height="349" src="https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/Canopy-Packages-min-1.png" class="vc_single_image-img attachment-large" alt="" srcset="https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/Canopy-Packages-min-1.png 400w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/Canopy-Packages-min-1-300x262.png 300w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/Canopy-Packages-min-1-125x109.png 125w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/Canopy-Packages-min-1-75x65.png 75w" sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px">
                                          </div>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <p style="text-align: center;"><em>Canopy provides easy access to over 450 Python 2 and Python 3 packages from the trusted Enthought Python Distribution</em></p>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 25px;"></div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                     <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6">
                                      <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                       <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <h3 class="p1">Canopy provides a complete, self-contained installer that gets you up and running with Python and a library of scientific and analytic tools  fast</h3>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 25px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <p>Canopy provides fast&nbsp;installation of both an interactive analysis environment plus the Python version of your choice (e.g. 2.7 or 3.5) and a core set of curated Python packages from the well-known Enthought Python Distribution.</p>
                                          <p>In just minutes, youll have a fully working Python environment with tools for common scientific and analytic programming workflows pre-installed: Jupyter, Matplotlib, NumPy and SciPy optimized with the latest Intel MKL, Matplotlib, Scikit-learn,&nbsp;and Pandas, plus instant access to over&nbsp;<a href="/product/canopy/#/package-index">450 additional pre-built and tested scientific and analytic packages</a>&nbsp;to customize your toolset.</p>
                                          <p>No command line, no complex multi-stage setups! (although if you do prefer a flat, standalone command line interface for package and environment management, we offer that via the&nbsp;<a href="/product/enthought-deployment-manager/">EDM tool</a>)</p>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                    </div>
                                   </div>
                                   <div class="separator  normal   " style="margin-top: 80px;margin-bottom: 80px;background-color: #b7b7b7;"></div>
                                   <div class="vc_row wpb_row section vc_row-fluid vc_inner " style=" text-align:left;">
                                    <div class=" full_section_inner clearfix">
                                     <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6">
                                      <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                       <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <h3 class="p1">Canopy provides access to a curated, quality assured set of packages managed through an intuitive graphical package manager with a state-of-the art dependency solver</h3>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 25px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <p>Our users cant afford to take chances with the stability of their software and applications, and using Canopy as their gateway to the Python ecosystem helps take the risk out of the wild west of open source software. Through Canopy, users can easily access both the most Enthought approved current stable version as well as historical versions of the libraries in the scientific Python stack.</p>
                                          <p>Plus, Canopy provides a graphical package manager to easily search, install, and remove packages from the user environment. The underlying EDM (Enthought Deployment Manager) back end takes care of complex dependency management to ensure nothing breaks in the process.</p>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>

                                          <p style="text-align: center;"><em>Canopys interactive analysis environment has powerful capabilities to go from data exploration through application development</em></p>
                                         </div>

                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <p style="text-align: center;"><em>Canopys&nbsp;interactive graphical debugger with variable browser&nbsp;helps you quickly find and fix code errors, understand and investigate code and data, and write new code more quickly</em></p>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                     <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6">
                                      <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                       <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <h3 class="p1">Canopys straightforward analysis environment is specifically tailored to the needs and workflows of scientists, analysts, and engineers</h3>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 25px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <p>Four integrated features of&nbsp;the Canopy analysis environment combine to create a powerful, yet streamlined platform: (1) a code editor, (2) an IPython window,&nbsp;(3) an interactive graphical debugger with variable browser, and (4) a data import tool.</p>
                                          <ul>
                                           <li>Canopys&nbsp;<strong>code editor</strong>&nbsp;comes with everything needed to explore and visualize data, without the burden of advanced development environments. Syntax highlighting, code auto-completion, and error checking allow users to quickly interact with Python code, write, and execute existing code.</li>
                                           <li>The integrated<strong>&nbsp;IPython window</strong>&nbsp;lets you quickly test code, experiment with ideas and see the results of code run directly from the editor. Canopy also includes pre-configured&nbsp;Jupyter Notebook access.</li>
                                           <li>Canopys&nbsp;<strong><a href="/product/canopy/#/canopy-interactive-debugger">interactive graphical debugger with variable browser</a></strong>&nbsp;helps you quickly find and fix code errors, understand and investigate code and data, and write new code more quickly.</li>
                                           <li>The built-in Canopy&nbsp;<a href="/product/canopy/#/canopy-data-import-tool"><strong>Data Import Tool</strong></a>&nbsp;helps you automate your data ingestion steps and automatically import tabular data files such as CSVs into Pandas DataFrames.</li>
                                          </ul>
                                          <p>Finally, access to package documentation at your fingertips in Canopy is a great benefit to faster coding, allowing you to easily extract and execute code to get started working quickly.</p>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                    </div>
                                   </div>
                                   <div class="separator  normal   " style="margin-top: 80px;margin-bottom: 80px;background-color: #b7b7b7;"></div>
                                   <div class="vc_row wpb_row section vc_row-fluid vc_inner " style=" text-align:left;">
                                    <div class=" full_section_inner clearfix">
                                     <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6">
                                      <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                       <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <h3 class="p1">Canopy is designed to be extensible for the enterprise</h3>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 25px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <p>Canopy not only provides a consistent Python toolset for all 3 major operating systems and support for a wide variety of use cases from data science and analysis to application development, but it is also extensible with other cross-enterprise tools, such with Excel via&nbsp;<a href="/product/pyxll">PyXLL</a>&nbsp;or with LabVIEW from National Instruments with the&nbsp;<a href="/product/python-for-labview/">Python Integration Toolkit for LabVIEW</a>.</p>
                                          <p>But it doesnt stop there. If an enterprise has Python embedded in another software application,&nbsp;Canopy can be directly connected to that application to provide coding and debugging capabilities. Canopy itself can even be customized or embedded to provide a sophisticated Python interface for your applications.&nbsp;<a href="/contact/">Contact us</a>&nbsp;to learn more about these options.</p>
                                          <p>Finally, in addition to accessing the libraries in the Enthought Python Distribution from Canopy, users can use the same tools to share and deploy their own internal, private packages by adding the&nbsp;<a href="/product/enthought-deployment-server/">Enthought Deployment Server</a>. &nbsp;The Enthought Deployment Server also allows enterprises to have a private, &nbsp;onsite copy of the full Enthought Python Distribution on their own approved servers and&nbsp;compliant with their existing security protocols.</p>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                     <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6">
                                      <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                       <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                        <div class="wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <div class="vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey">
                                           <img width="300" height="98" src="https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16-300x98.png" class="vc_single_image-img attachment-medium" alt="" srcset="https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16-300x98.png 300w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16-768x252.png 768w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16-1024x336.png 1024w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16-125x41.png 125w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16-75x25.png 75w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16-700x230.png 700w, https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/PyXLL-Logo-03.16.16.png 1159w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px">
                                          </div>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <p style="text-align: center;"><em>When combined with <a href="/product/pyxll">PyXLL</a>, Canopy provides a Python interface to build powerful algorithms and dashboards in Excel</em></p>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 40px;margin-bottom: 40px;"></div>

                     <div id="tab-canopy-data-import-tool" class="tab-content">
                      <div class="vc_row wpb_row section vc_row-fluid vc_inner " style=" text-align:left;">
                       <div class=" full_section_inner clearfix">
                        <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12">
                         <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                          <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                           <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                            <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                             <div class="vc_row wpb_row section vc_row-fluid " style="background-color:#ffffff; padding-top:25px; padding-bottom:10px; text-align:left;">
                              <div class=" full_section_inner clearfix">
                               <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12">
                                <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                 <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                  <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                   <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                    <h2 style="text-align: center;">Canopy Data Import Tool</h2>
                                   </div>
                                  </div>
                                 </div>
                                </div>
                               </div>
                              </div>
                             </div>
                             <div class="vc_row wpb_row section vc_row-fluid " style="background-color:#ffffff; padding-top:10px; padding-bottom:30px; text-align:left;">
                              <div class=" full_section_inner clearfix">
                               <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8">
                                <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                 <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                  <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                   <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                    <p style="text-align: left;">The Canopy Data Import Tool allows you to import and manipulate CSV and&nbsp;columnar text data files in an easy, reproducible way.</p>
                                    <p style="text-align: left;">It is built on top of Pandas, providing an exploratory, graphical interface&nbsp;for data manipulation while still using a familiar Python representation of your data. Once you have cleaned your data, you can take control of the underlying data frame. You can also export a Python (Pandas) script of the commands that you used, so that you can perform those same manipulations again.</p>
                                    <p>The Data Import Tool is a Canopy subscriber-exclusive feature. <a href="/product/canopy/#/subscribe">Subscribe today</a> to get access!</p>
                                   </div>
                                  </div>
                                 </div>
                                </div>
                               </div>
                               <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4">
                                <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                 <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                  <div class="wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center">
                                   <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                    <div class="vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey">
                                     <img class="vc_single_image-img " src="https://ljibmsizre1tbaub4bl15j18-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/canopy-data-import-tool-icon-white-removed-01-250x205.png" width="250" height="205" alt="canopy-data-import-tool-icon-white-removed-01" title="canopy-data-import-tool-icon-white-removed-01">
                                    </div>

                                         <h2 class="p1" style="text-align: left;">Benefits of the Canopy Data Import Tool</h2>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                       <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 10px;"></div>
                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1"><span class="number-circle">1</span> Easily import your data from structured text files, URLs containing embedded tables, or from your clipboards</span></p>
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1"><span class="number-circle">2</span> View and manipulate data in the Pandas DataFrame while simultaneously capturing the corresponding the Python code</span></p>
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1"><span class="number-circle">3</span> Create re-usable recipes for common data munging tasks to expedite future data cleanup</span></p>
                                        </div>

                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <h2 class="p1" style="text-align: center;">Reduce Time Spent on Data Analysis with the Canopy Data Import Tool</h2>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                       <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 10px;"></div>
                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <p>Whether you are a data scientist, quantitative analyst, or an&nbsp;engineer, or if&nbsp;you are evaluating consumer purchase behavior, stock portfolios, or design simulation&nbsp;results, your data analysis workflow probably looks a lot like this:</p>
                                         <p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Acquire &gt; Wrangle</strong> &gt; Analyze and Model &gt; Share and Refine &gt; Publish</p>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                    </div>
                                   </div>
                                  </div>
                                  <div class="vc_row wpb_row section vc_row-fluid vc_inner " style=" text-align:left;">
                                   <div class=" full_section_inner clearfix">
                                    <div class="number-outdent wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6">
                                     <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                      <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <p>The problem is that often 50 to 80 percent of time is spent wading through the tedium of the first two steps  <strong>acquiring and wrangling data</strong>  before even getting to the real work of analysis and insight.</p>
                                         <p><strong>In this webinar we demonstrate&nbsp;how the Canopy Data Import Tool&nbsp;can&nbsp;</strong><strong>significantly reduce the time you spend on data analysis dirty work,</strong> by helping you:</p>
                                         <ul>
                                          <li>Load various data file types and URLs containing embedded tables into Pandas DataFrames</li>
                                          <li>Perform data munging tasks that improve raw data</li>
                                          <li>Handle complicated and/or messy data</li>
                                          <li>Extend the work done with the tool to other data files</li>
                                         </ul>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                       <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 20px;"></div>

                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <h3 class="p1"><span class="number-circle">1</span> Interactive DataFrame View</h3>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                       <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1">The DataFrame View is used to view the data and perform basic manipulations. Cells can be edited by double-clicking on them, with each cells editor corresponding to its column type. For example, a date/time column uses a time and calendar editor widget. Many transformations can be accessed by right-clicking on a column or row. The rest can be accessed through the Transforms menu.</span></p>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                    </div>
                                   </div>
                                  </div>

                                     <div class="vc_column-inner ">
                                      <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <h3 class="p1"><span class="number-circle">2</span> Command History</h3>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                       <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1">As commands are executed they are logged in a visible command history stack. This allows you to see the exact steps that have been taken while you transform your data.</span></p>
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1">Commands in the command history can be enabled, disabled, or removed. These operations can be done to a command at any point in the history, and the other commands in the history will be reverted and re-executed accordingly to ensure that all commands are performed correctly.</span></p>
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1">Once you have completed your data cleanup, you can:</span></p>
                                         <ul>
                                          <li>Export to a DataFrame to used in the IPython console</li>
                                          <li>Save scripts to reproduce actions on other datasets</li>
                                         </ul>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                      </div>
                                     </div>
                                    </div>
                                   </div>

                                     <div class="vc_column-inner ">

                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <h3 class="p1"><span class="number-circle">3</span> Data View Options</h3>
                                        </div>
                                       </div>
                                       <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                       <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
                                        <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                         <p class="p1"><span class="s1">As you issue commands and manipulate your data, the tool records these actions in the form of Python / Pandas code that can be exported for reuse later, potentially on other datasets. This view is read-only.</span></p>

                                   <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  skinny">
                                    <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                     <p style="text-align: center;">Enthought Canopys interactive graphical Python debugger has powerful functionality to help you quickly find and fix code errors, understand and investigate code, and write new code more quickly.</p>
                                    </div>

                                          <p class="p1"><span class="s1">The integrated debugger, together with Canopys advanced text editor with syntax highlighting, Python code auto-completion, and error checking, provides a robust development tool that makes solving complex coding issues easier and supports more accurate, efficient, and maintainable code development.</span></p>

                                          <ul>
                                           <li>Displays variables and watch expressions in the currently selected frame of the Stack Browser pane as you step through code</li>
                                           <li>Easily identifiable color-coding of function parameters, function return values, exceptions, and watch expressions</li>
                                           <li>Allows for direct inline editing of select variables</li>
                                           <li>Shows a high level view of all selected variables in the upper pane</li>
                                           <li>Drill down into type-specific detailed representation of the content in the lower pane</li>
                                           <li>View user custom-defined variables from the Python pane when not debugging</li>
                                          </ul>

                                          <ul>
                                           <li class="p1">Easily navigate a complex execution stack as you step through code</li>
                                           <li class="p1">Shows you the frame stack of the debugged program when it is paused at a breakpoint or when stepping through code</li>
                                           <li class="p1">Click on any frame in the stack to show its local variables in the Variable Browser pane</li>
                                           <li class="p1">Double click on any frame in the stack to open the corresponding line of code in the code editor</li>

                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <section class="row">
                                           <div class="span12 likeTable">
                                            <ul>
                                             <li>Shows all defined breakpoints in a single pane (places in the code where you want to temporarily pause execution to inspect the running program)</li>
                                             <li>Allows you to easily enable/disable breakpoints or edit breakpoint conditions</li>
                                            </ul>

                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  skinny">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <h3 class="p1"><span class="number-circle">4</span> IPython Pane Integration</h3>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  skinny">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <section class="row">
                                           <div class="span12 likeTable">
                                            <ul>
                                             <li>Tight integration, so that changes in the Canopy debugger are reflected in the IPython debugger, and vice versa</li>
                                             <li>Allows you to interact with data values or even call functions while paused in the live execution of your code. This helps you understand your code and data more deeply, and provides a powerful way to experiment with alternative approaches to the desired solution</li>
                                             <li>Take advantage of the full interactive power and flexibility of the IPython command-line environment when your program is paused</li>
                                             <li>Integration with IPython allows for interactive coding and data manipulation with ability to view plots, graphs, and arrays directly in the IPython pane using popular packages such as matplotlib, scikit-image, plot.ly and more</li>
                                             <li>Canopy debugger commands map directly to IPython debugging commands, for an easy learning curve</li>
                                            </ul>
                                           </div>
                                          </section>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>

                                          <h3 class="p1"><span class="number-circle">5</span> Canopy Code Editor</h3>
                                         </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="separator  transparent   " style="margin-top: 25px;margin-bottom: 0px;"></div>
                                        <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  skinny">
                                         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                                          <section class="row">
                                           <div class="span12 likeTable">
                                            <ul>
                                             <li>Canopys code editor includes static syntax highlighting, Python code auto-completion, and error checking</li>
                                             <li>The integrated debugger enhances the editor by providing floating tooltips to show you the value of active variables in the editor, while debugging</li>
                                            </ul>
